HTTP is the foundation of the web, allowing different systems to communicate with each other and exchange information. This protocol is used to request and display web pages, as well as to send data from a user's browser to a server.

It is a fundamental protocol used for transferring data, including web pages, over the internet. HTTP is the foundation of the web, allowing different systems to communicate with each other and exchange information. In web addresses, HTTP is often preceded by "http://" or "https://" (the secure version of the protocol), which indicates the protocol being used to access the website. For example, in the URL "https://fortune.com/2024/11/04/harris-trump-victory-the-markets-unless-winner-sweeps-congress/", "https" is the protocol used to access the website (Source 8).
